1. EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
The Vision

Enterprise 11 establishes the Carbon Infinity Loop — a fully circular, net-negative carbon enterprise that transforms atmospheric CO₂ and organic waste into permanent high-value materials through lab-grown diamonds and advanced graphene. This enterprise serves as the technological catalyst for the entire EVER (EcoVille Enterprise Residence) network, enabling advanced manufacturing capabilities across all sister enterprises while permanently sequestering carbon in valuable products.
Core Innovation

2. PURPOSE CRYSTALLIZATION
Core Purpose Statement

    Transform atmospheric carbon and organic waste into permanent high-value materials through 100% renewable processes, achieving net-negative emissions while providing equidistributed economic benefits, serving as technological catalyst for regenerative enterprise networks, and demonstrating that industrial excellence and environmental regeneration are not just compatible but synergistic.

Optimal Definition

OPTIBEST for Enterprise 11 means achieving the simultaneous maximum of:

    Carbon sequestration per unit input — Every gram of input carbon permanently stored
    Value creation from captured carbon — Maximum economic value from permanent storage
    Complete circularity — Zero waste, infinite loops
    Energy self-sufficiency — 100% renewable, net-positive capability
    Seamless scalability — From prototype to planetary scale without redesign
    Full EFE compatibility — Equidistributed, accessible, free
    Network amplification — Each enterprise enhanced by E11 integration

3. CONSTRAINT LIBERATION
Convention Mapping
Domain Convention	Current Limitation	Liberation Approach	Result
Natural gas CVD feedstock	Fossil carbon dependence	Bio-methane + DAC CO₂	100% renewable carbon
Centralized diamond production	High transport costs, limited access	Distributed modular facilities	Global accessibility
Diamonds as luxury products	Limited market, high margins only	247+ industrial applications	Mass market + premium
Graphene separate from diamond	Inefficient parallel production	Integrated diamond-graphene hub	Synergistic production
Linear production model	Waste generation, resource depletion	Infinite circularity loops	Zero waste
Proprietary technology	Limited accessibility, monopolies	Open-source protocols	Global replication

Constraint Inversion Protocol

Every Constraint Becomes a Feature:
Original Constraint	Inverted Feature
CVD requires high energy	Heat recovery powers DAC regeneration
Diamond growth is slow	Extended growth → higher quality → premium pricing
Graphene production creates waste	Diamond waste becomes graphene feedstock
Multiple reactor types needed	Modular design allows specialized production
Quality control is complex	AI monitoring creates data for process optimization
Carbon tracking is difficult	Blockchain passport creates premium product identity

System Integration Matrix

text

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
                    SYSTEM INTEGRATION MATRIX
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

                    │ DAC │ CARB│ BIO │ CVD │ LASER│ SORT│ PROC│ CIRC│
────────────────────┼─────┼─────┼─────┼─────┼──────┼─────┼─────┼─────┤
DAC (CO₂ Capture)   │  █  │  →  │  →  │  →  │      │     │     │     │
CARB (Carbonize)    │     │  █  │  →  │  →  │      │     │     │  ←  │
BIO (Bio-Methane)   │     │  ←  │  █  │  →  │      │     │     │     │
CVD (Diamond)       │  ←  │  ←  │  ←  │  █  │  →   │  →  │     │  ←  │
LASER (Graphene)    │     │     │     │  ←  │  █   │     │  →  │  ←  │
SORT (AI Grading)   │     │     │     │     │      │  █  │  →  │  →  │
PROC (Processing)   │     │     │     │     │  ←   │  ←  │  █  │  →  │
CIRC (Circularity)  │     │  →  │     │  →  │  →   │  ←  │  ←  │  █  │

LEGEND:
█  = System self
→  = Provides output to
←  = Receives input from

INTEGRATION DENSITY: 94% (28/30 possible connections active)

                    DIRECT AIR CAPTURE SYSTEM

TECHNOLOGY: Next-Generation Solid Sorbent DAC with Integrated Thermal Recovery

PERFORMANCE SPECIFICATIONS:
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Parameter              │ Specification            │ Benchmark vs. Industry  │

│ Energy consumption     │ 1,650 kWh/ton CO₂        │ 18% below industry avg  │
│ Purity                 │ 99.99%                   │ Matches best available  │

│ Availability           │ 95%                      │ Industry standard       │
│ Footprint              │ 2.2 hectares             │ 15% more compact        │

│   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
└──────────────────────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────┘
                                       │
                                       ▼
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                          SORBENT CONTACTOR ARRAY                             │
│                                                                              │
│   ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    │
│   │                    24 MODULAR CONTACTORS                           │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   ┌──────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────┐ │    │
│   │   │    CONTACTOR 1   │  │    CONTACTOR 2   │  │    CONTACTOR 3   │ │    │
│   │   │                  │  │                  │  │                  │ │    │
│   │   │  ┌────────────┐  │  │  ┌────────────┐  │  │  ┌────────────┐  │ │    │
│   │   │  │████████████│  │  │  │████████████│  │  │  │████████████│  │ │    │
│   │   │  │████████████│  │  │  │████████████│  │  │  │████████████│  │ │    │
│   │   │  │  AMINE     │  │  │  │  AMINE     │  │  │  │  AMINE     │  │ │    │
│   │   │  │  SORBENT   │  │  │  │  SORBENT   │  │  │  │  SORBENT   │  │ │    │
│   │   │  │  BED       │  │  │  │  BED       │  │  │  │  BED       │  │ │    │
│   │   │  │████████████│  │  │  │████████████│  │  │  │████████████│  │ │    │
│   │   │  └────────────┘  │  │  └────────────┘  │  │  └────────────┘  │ │    │
│   │   │                  │  │                  │  │                  │ │    │
│   │   │  Status: ADSORB  │  │  Status: REGEN   │  │  Status: COOL    │ │    │
│   │   └──────────────────┘  └──────────────────┘  └──────────────────┘ │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   ... (24 contactors in rotating 3-phase cycle)                    │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   CYCLE PHASES:                                                    │    │
│   │   ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │    │
│   │   │ Phase 1: ADSORPTION (8 units active)                         │ │    │
│   │   │   • Air flow through sorbent bed                             │ │    │
│   │   │   • CO₂ chemically binds to amine groups                     │ │    │
│   │   │   • Duration: 60 minutes                                     │ │    │
│   │   │   • Capacity: ~90% CO₂ capture from inlet                    │ │    │
│   │   ├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤ │    │
│   │   │ Phase 2: REGENERATION (8 units active)                       │ │    │
│   │   │   • Thermal input: 85-120°C (solar thermal)                  │ │    │
│   │   │   • CO₂ released from saturated sorbent                      │ │    │
│   │   │   • Duration: 45 minutes                                     │ │    │
│   │   │   • Purity: 99.99% CO₂                                       │ │    │
│   │   ├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤ │    │
│   │   │ Phase 3: COOLING (8 units active)                            │ │    │
│   │   │   • Heat recovery to thermal storage                         │ │    │
│   │   │   • Cool to ambient for next adsorption                      │ │    │
│   │   │   • Duration: 30 minutes                                     │ │    │
│   │   │   • Energy recovery: 78%                                     │ │    │
│   │   └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │    │
│   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                       │
                                       ▼
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                          THERMAL REGENERATION SYSTEM                         │
│                                                                              │
│   ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    │
│   │                    HEAT SOURCE INTEGRATION                         │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   ┌─────────────────┐                                              │    │
│   │   │  SOLAR THERMAL  │───────────────────┐                         │    │
│   │   │   (PRIMARY)     │                   │                         │    │
│   │   │   2.5 MW peak   │                   │                         │    │
│   │   │   Parabolic     │                   │                         │    │
│   │   │   trough array  │                   │                         │    │
│   │   └─────────────────┘                   │                         │    │
│   │                                         │                         │    │
│   │   ┌─────────────────┐                   ▼                         │    │
│   │   │  CVD HEAT       │─────────→ ┌─────────────────┐               │    │
│   │   │  RECOVERY       │          │   THERMAL       │               │    │
│   │   │   (SECONDARY)   │          │   MANIFOLD      │──→ 85-120°C   │    │
│   │   │   1.2 MW        │          │                 │    to sorbent │    │
│   │   │   Waste heat    │─────────→│   Temperature   │               │    │
│   │   └─────────────────┘          │   regulation    │               │    │
│   │                                │   + buffering   │               │    │
│   │   ┌─────────────────┐          └─────────────────┘               │    │
│   │   │  THERMAL        │                   ▲                         │    │
│   │   │  STORAGE        │───────────────────┘                         │    │
│   │   │   (BACKUP)      │                                             │    │
│   │   │   50 MWh        │                                             │    │
│   │   │   Molten salt   │                                             │    │
│   │   └─────────────────┘                                             │    │
│   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                       │
                                       ▼
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                          CO₂ PURIFICATION & COMPRESSION                      │
│                                                                              │
│   ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   Raw CO₂ ──→ Dehumidify ──→ Filter ──→ Compress ──→ Store        │    │
│   │   (from         (desiccant)   (activated   (multi-     (200 bar   │    │
│   │   regen)                       carbon)     stage)      buffer)    │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   SPECIFICATIONS:                                                  │    │
│   │   • Input: ~17 tons CO₂/day (variable with weather)               │    │
│   │   • Output: 99.99% pure CO₂                                       │    │
│   │   • Compression: 4-stage with intercooling                        │    │
│   │   • Energy: 120 kWh/ton CO₂ (compression only)                    │    │
│   │   • Buffer storage: 50 tons CO₂ (3-day reserve)                   │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    │
│                                                                              │
│   OUTPUT TO CVD:                                                            │
│   ┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    │
│   │   CO₂ (99.99%) → Catalytic Conversion → CH₄ (bio-methane blend)   │    │
│   │                   (Sabatier reactor)    + H₂ supplement            │    │
│   │                                                                     │    │
│   │   Path 1: Direct to bio-methane reformer                          │    │
│   │   Path 2: Storage for carbon credit verification                   │    │
│   │   Path 3: External sale (if excess capacity)                       │    │
│   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

│   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                             │
│   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
│   TOTAL CARBON OUTPUT:       6,321 t C/year (balanced)                    │
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

                              NET CARBON BALANCE
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                                                                             │
│   CALCULATION:                                                             │
│   ────────────                                                             │
│                                                                             │
│   Carbon captured from atmosphere:                                         │
│     DAC CO₂ capture:               +6,200 t CO₂                           │
│                                                                             │
│   Carbon captured from waste (avoided emissions):                          │
│     Organic waste diversion:       +13,933 t CO₂e                         │
│     (would have decomposed aerobically, releasing methane)                 │
│                                                                             │
│   Carbon permanently stored:                                               │
│     In diamond products:           -6.6 t CO₂e (permanent)                │
│     In graphene products:          -1.9 t CO₂e (permanent)                │
│     In biochar (soil):             -9,166 t CO₂e (1000+ years)            │
│                                                                             │
│   Operational emissions:                                                   │
│     Transport (electric vehicles): +120 t CO₂e                            │
│     Equipment (maintenance):       +30 t CO₂e                              │
│     TOTAL OPERATIONAL:             +150 t CO₂e                             │
│                                                                             │
│   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════  │
│                                                                             │
│   NET ANNUAL CARBON effect:                                                │
│                                                                             │
│   Captured:     6,200 + 13,933     = +20,133 t CO₂e                       │
│   Stored:       6.6 + 1.9 + 9,166  = -9,175 t CO₂e                        │
│   Emitted:                         = +150 t CO₂e                           │
│                                                                             │
│   NET BALANCE:  20,133 - 9,175 - 150 = -8,408 t CO₂e/year                │
│                                                                             │
│                        ╔═══════════════════════════╗                       │
│                        ║   CARBON NEGATIVE ✓       ║                       │
│                        ║   -8,400 t CO₂e/year      ║                       │
│                        ╚═══════════════════════════╝                       │
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

│   │                                                                      │  │

│   │   │   ├── Concentrated solar power (CSP) integration           │    │  │
│   │   │   ├── Minimal water DAC variants                           │    │  │
│   │   │   ├── Enhanced dust protection                             │    │  │
│   │   │   ├── Reduced organic feedstock (more DAC focus)           │    │  │
│   │   │   └── Thermal desalination integration                     │    │  │
│   │   │                                                             │    │  │
│   │   │   REGIONS: Middle East, Sahara, Australian Outback,        │    │  │
│   │   │            Atacama, Southwestern USA                        │    │  │
│   │   │                                                             │    │  │
│   │   │   ADVANTAGES:                                               │    │  │
│   │   │   ├── Highest solar irradiance globally                    │    │  │
│   │   │   ├── Low humidity (better for DAC)                        │    │  │
│   │   │   ├── Minimal weather disruption                           │    │  │
│   │   │   └── Abundant land availability                           │    │  │

Regional Adaptation Matrix
Factor	Tropical	Temperate	Arid	Cold	Coastal
Solar PV	High yield	Standard	Highest	Variable	Moderate
Wind	Moderate	Good	Variable	Excellent	Excellent
DAC Efficiency	Lower	Standard	Higher	Highest	Standard
Organic Waste	Abundant	Seasonal	Limited	Limited	Moderate
Cooling Needs	High	Medium	Highest	Low	Medium
Heating Needs	None	Medium	Low	High	Low
Capital Modifier	+5%	Baseline	+10%	+15%	+8%

Aequchain Smart Contracts

text

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
                    SMART CONTRACT SUITE
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                                                                             │
│   CONTRACT 1: MATERIAL PASSPORT                                            │
│   ═══════════════════════════════                                           │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   // MaterialPassport.sol                                           │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   FUNCTIONS:                                                        │  │
│   │   ├── createPassport(materialData, carbonSource, quality)          │  │
│   │   │   → Creates new passport on production                         │  │
│   │   │   → Immutable origin data                                      │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── updateCascadeStage(passportId, newStage, assessmentData)     │  │
│   │   │   → Records cascade progression                                │  │
│   │   │   → AI assessment data stored                                  │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── transferOwnership(passportId, newOwner, transferData)        │  │
│   │   │   → Records ownership changes                                  │  │
│   │   │   → Maintains full chain of custody                            │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── verifyPassport(passportId)                                   │  │
│   │   │   → Returns full passport data                                 │  │
│   │   │   → Includes verification hash                                 │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   └── linkCarbonCredit(passportId, creditId)                       │  │
│   │       → Associates verified carbon credit                          │  │
│   │       → Cross-references with credit registry                      │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   EVENTS:                                                           │  │
│   │   ├── PassportCreated(passportId, creator, timestamp)              │  │
│   │   ├── StageUpdated(passportId, oldStage, newStage)                 │  │
│   │   ├── OwnershipTransferred(passportId, from, to)                   │  │
│   │   └── CreditLinked(passportId, creditId)                           │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                             │
│   CONTRACT 2: EQUIDISTRIBUTED PROFIT                                       │
│   ══════════════════════════════════                                        │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   // EquidistributedProfit.sol                                      │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   FUNCTIONS:                                                        │  │
│   │   ├── recordRevenue(amount, source, timestamp)                     │  │
│   │   │   → Records all incoming revenue                               │  │
│   │   │   → Categorized by source                                      │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── recordExpense(amount, category, recipient)                   │  │
│   │   │   → Records all outgoing expenses                              │  │
│   │   │   → Full audit trail                                           │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── calculateProfitShare(period)                                 │  │
│   │   │   → Computes available profit                                  │  │
│   │   │   → Applies allocation formula                                 │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── distributeProfitShare()                                      │  │
│   │   │   → Executes quarterly distribution                            │  │
│   │   │   → Equal share to all eligible employees                      │  │
│   │   │   → Automatic fund allocations                                 │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   └── auditFinancials(startDate, endDate)                          │  │
│   │       → Returns complete financial record                          │  │
│   │       → Third-party verifiable                                     │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   ALLOCATION FORMULA (Hardcoded):                                   │  │
│   │   ├── 40% → Employee Profit Share (equal per person)               │  │
│   │   ├── 30% → Reinvestment Reserve                                   │  │
│   │   ├── 20% → EVER Network Fund                                      │  │
│   │   └── 10% → Community Benefit Fund                                 │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   GOVERNANCE:                                                       │  │
│   │   ├── Formula changes require 75% employee vote                    │  │
│   │   ├── All transactions publicly auditable                          │  │
│   │   └── Real-time profit tracking visible to all                     │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                             │
│   CONTRACT 3: CARBON CREDIT REGISTRY                                       │
│   ══════════════════════════════════                                        │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   // CarbonCreditRegistry.sol                                       │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   FUNCTIONS:                                                        │  │
│   │   ├── registerCapture(source, amount, verificationData)            │  │
│   │   │   → Records carbon capture event                               │  │
│   │   │   → Links to monitoring data                                   │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── requestVerification(captureId)                               │  │
│   │   │   → Initiates third-party verification                         │  │
│   │   │   → Oracle integration with Verra/Gold Standard                │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── issueCredit(captureId, verificationProof)                    │  │
│   │   │   → Mints verified carbon credit token                         │  │
│   │   │   → Links to material passport if applicable                   │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── transferCredit(creditId, recipient)                          │  │
│   │   │   → Enables credit trading                                     │  │
│   │   │   → Maintains full provenance                                  │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── retireCredit(creditId, retirementReason)                     │  │
│   │   │   → Permanently removes from circulation                       │  │
│   │   │   → Records offset claim                                       │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   └── queryCredits(filters)                                        │  │
│   │       → Returns credit data based on criteria                      │  │
│   │       → Supports carbon market integration                         │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   CREDIT TYPES:                                                     │  │
│   │   ├── DAC_CAPTURE: Direct air capture credits                      │  │
│   │   ├── WASTE_DIVERSION: Avoided emissions from waste                │  │
│   │   ├── BIOCHAR_STORAGE: Soil carbon sequestration                   │  │
│   │   └── PRODUCT_STORAGE: Permanent storage in products               │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                             │
│   CONTRACT 4: CROSS-ENTERPRISE TRANSACTIONS                                │
│   ══════════════════════════════════════════                                │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   // CrossEnterpriseTransactions.sol                                │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   FUNCTIONS:                                                        │  │
│   │   ├── createOrder(fromEnterprise, toEnterprise, items, terms)      │  │
│   │   │   → Initiates cross-enterprise order                           │  │
│   │   │   → Smart contract escrow                                      │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── fulfillOrder(orderId, deliveryProof)                         │  │
│   │   │   → Confirms delivery                                          │  │
│   │   │   → Releases payment                                           │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── disputeOrder(orderId, disputeData)                           │  │
│   │   │   → Initiates dispute resolution                               │  │
│   │   │   → Arbitration by EVER network                                │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   └── settleNetPositions(period)                                   │  │
│   │       → Calculates net flows between enterprises                   │  │
│   │       → Minimizes actual transfers                                 │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   INTER-ENTERPRISE PRICING:                                         │  │
│   │   ├── Cost-plus model (transparent margins)                        │  │
│   │   ├── Volume discounts for network members                         │  │
│   │   └── Priority allocation for EVER enterprises                     │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                             │
│   CONTRACT 5: GOVERNANCE                                                   │
│   ══════════════════════                                                    │
│                                                                             │
│   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   // EnterpriseGovernance.sol                                       │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   FUNCTIONS:                                                        │  │
│   │   ├── createProposal(title, description, proposalType)             │  │
│   │   │   → Any employee can propose                                   │  │
│   │   │   → Minimum discussion period                                  │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── vote(proposalId, vote, justification)                        │  │
│   │   │   → One employee, one vote                                     │  │
│   │   │   → Optional justification for transparency                    │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   ├── executeProposal(proposalId)                                  │  │
│   │   │   → Automatic execution if passed                              │  │
│   │   │   → Time-locked for safety                                     │  │
│   │   │                                                                  │  │
│   │   └── delegateVote(delegateTo)                                     │  │
│   │       → Optional delegation                                        │  │
│   │       → Revocable at any time                                      │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   │   PROPOSAL TYPES & THRESHOLDS:                                      │  │
│   │   ├── Operational (minor): 50% + 1                                 │  │
│   │   ├── Strategic (major): 66%                                       │  │
│   │   ├── Constitutional (fundamental): 75%                            │  │
│   │   └── Emergency: 90% (immediate execution)                         │  │
│   │                                                                      │  │
│   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Aequchain Integration Specifications
Component	Specification	Purpose
Node Type	Full node + Archive	Complete data access
Sync Mode	Fast sync + State pruning	Efficient storage
API	GraphQL + REST	Flexible integration
Authentication	Multi-signature	Security
Backup	Real-time replication	Data integrity
Uptime Target	99.99%	Reliability
Transaction Cost	Minimal (PoS)	Cost efficiency

│      stores atmospheric carbon. Every operation captures more CO₂          │
│      than it could possibly emit.                                          │

│   carbon captured, by lives improved, by knowledge shared.                 │
